Their core product is a dispatching solution that uses artificial intelligence to optimize the assignment of technicians to service calls. The software aims to increase revenue by sending the \\\"right tech to the right call\\\" based on historical data and expected sales performance. It also focuses on improving operational efficiency for dispatchers and enhancing the customer experience.\\n\\nProbook offers two main product tiers:\\n1.  **Copilot:** This level provides recommendations for dispatchers, allowing them to make right-tech, right-call decisions with the click of a button. It includes real-time syncing with ServiceTitan and keeps dispatchers informed with recommendations.\\n2.  **Autopilot:** This is a higher level of automation that fully reshuffles the dispatch board in real-time. Their target users within these companies are dispatchers, operations managers, general managers, and company presidents/owners.\\n\\nWho founded the company:\\nThe CEO is George Eliadis. No other founders are explicitly mentioned.\\n\\nOther important facts about the company, if mentioned (such as headquarters location, year founded, funding status, notable milestones, or any distinguishing features):\\nProbook offers a 2-day in-person launch with their CEO.\\nThey provide customer service with a 3-minute median response time, 25-minute median resolution time, and 100% post-resolution satisfaction.\\nThey integrate with ServiceTitan in real-time.\\nThey offer two levels of automation: Copilot and Autopilot.\\nThey were founded by dispatchers, for dispatchers.\\nThey offer a live updating Revenue Heatmap.\\nThey track sales through the install process to accurately credit technicians.\\nThey dynamically weigh windshield time based on call volume.\\nThey forecast how long techs will take at each call using historical data.\\nThey provide visibility into average revenue and job count by zip code.\\nThey allow setting thresholds for specific trades, job types, and tag bundles.\\nThey offer weekly check-in meetings and 24/7 on-call support post-launch.\\n\\nDetailed descriptions of the company's business model, products, services, and market positioning:\\nProbook's business model is centered around providing AI-powered dispatching software to home services companies. Their core product is a dispatching solution that uses artificial intelligence to optimize the assignment of technicians to service calls. The software aims to increase revenue by sending the \\\"right tech to the right call\\\" based on historical data and expected sales performance. It also focuses on improving operational efficiency for dispatchers and enhancing the customer experience.\\n\\nProbook offers two main product tiers:\\n1.  **Copilot:** This level provides recommendations for dispatchers, allowing them to make right-tech, right-call decisions with the click of a button. It includes real-time syncing with ServiceTitan and keeps dispatchers informed with recommendations.\\n2.  **Autopilot:** This is a higher level of automation that fully reshuffles the dispatch board in real-time. Dispatchers remain engaged by verifying job parameters, and this level is designed to allow a single dispatcher to manage 20-25+ technicians efficiently.\\n\\nKey services and features provided by Probook include:\\n-   **AI Dispatching:** Using AI to match technicians to jobs based on factors like expected sales performance, drive time, and technician skills.\\n-   **Revenue Maximization:** Optimizing dispatch decisions to increase average ticket size and flip rates (conversion of service calls to sales leads or installations).\\n-   **Efficiency Improvements:** Reducing dispatcher workload, allowing them to manage more technicians and freeing up time for customer service.
